This report shows that human \u03b2-defensins are also chemotactic for immature dendritic cells and memory T cells. Human \u03b2-defensin was selectively chemotactic for cells stably transfected to express human CCR6, a chemokine receptor preferentially expressed by immature dendritic cells and memory T cells. The \u03b2-defensin\u2013induced chemotaxis was sensitive to pertussis toxin and inhibited by antibodies to CCR6. The binding of iodinated LARC, the chemokine ligand for CCR6, to CCR6-transfected cells was competitively displaced by \u03b2-defensin.
